# Snow Machine

# Description __

A machine which will blanket the surrounding terrain in snow.

Page views: 4,035  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Stone Spear

# Description __

A stone-tipped wooden Spear. Slightly longer range.

Page views: 5,536  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Wooden Spear

# Description __

Primitive weapon, perfect for hunting your foes. Can be upgraded to Stone Spear.

Page views: 6,097  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Spider Webs

# Description __

Giant Cobwebs which can be hung against both a ceiling and a wall.

Page views: 5,441  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Wooden Floor Spikes

# Description __

A set of spikes that will slow down and hurt anyone that walks over them.

Page views: 5,242  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Small Stash

# Description __

A hidden, burried stash to keep your items safe. After placing, return to the stash and aim at the ground where you hid it and it will reveal itself.

Page views: 6,851  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Small Stocking

# Description __

A small stocking. Hang it by a fire and you might just get a gift! Collect 6 to upgrade to a SUPER Stocking.

Page views: 2,820  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/stone.pickaxe~history)



# Stone Pickaxe

# Description __

Primitive tool used for harvesting Stone, Metal ore and Sulfur ore.

This tool is an early game version of the [Pickaxe](/rust/item/pickaxe) and does not gather as efficiently.

Page views: 5,776  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/stonehatchet~history)



# Stone Hatchet

# Description __

Primitive tool used for harvesting wood from trees and logs. Can also harvest flesh from animals and players.

This tool is an early game version of the [Hatchet](/rust/item/hatchet) and does not gather as efficiently.

Page views: 6,045  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Stones

# Description __

Harvested from rocks using tools, basic building material.

Page views: 3,566  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Strobe Light

# Description __

A flashing light, 3 speeds. Causes seizures.

Page views: 4,660  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Sulfur

# Description __

Sulfur is commonly used in gunpowder, medicine, and matches. Matches release sulfur dioxide when they burn, giving them their smell. Sulfur is an essential component to living cells. Many proteins contain sulfur. It is also used as a pesticide on organic farms.

Page views: 3,825  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Sulfur Ore

# Description __

A rock containing sulfur. The sulfur can be extracted using a furnace.

Page views: 3,477  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Survey Charge

# Description __

Use this on the terrain to see which resources are available for mining.

Page views: 10,325  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

[Home](/rust/) / [Medical Syringe](/rust/item/syringe.medical)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/syringe.medical)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/syringe.medical~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/syringe.medical~history)



# Medical Syringe

# Description __

Heal yourself or others with this syringe. Left-click heals you, right-click heals a target. It gives +15 health.

Healing  
---  
+15 Health  
Does not stop bleeding  
Crafting  
---  
15 Cloth  
10 Metal Fragments  
10 Low Grade Fuel  
  
#### It takes 20 seconds to craft one syringe.__

Page views: 6,503  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Table

# Description __

Every home needs a table. A decorative item which provides comfort when in close proximity.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x100 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x50 Wood



Page views: 3,394  
Updated: This Year

# Tactical Gloves

# Description __

Military issue tactical gloves provide protection as well as weapon stabilization leading to higher accuracy when used.

Page views: 10,286  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Reactive Target

# Description __

A reactive target that knocks down when hit, can be reset.

Page views: 2,758  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Targeting Computer

# Description __

A computer loaded with software that can analyze a video and produce rotational deltas to individual objects contained in the feed.

Page views: 4,345  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Binoculars

# Description __

Binoculars allowing you to see objects at great length.

Page views: 5,159  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Camera

# Description __

A camera. Take screenshots with primary fire, zoom in and out with secondary fire, and lock focus with third fire.

Page views: 5,141  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Garry's Mod Tool Gun

# Description __

Celebrating 15 Years of Garry's Mod! Use this tool gun to upgrade building parts. Right-click for the options. You can also pick up deployed objects while the hammer is equipped.

Page views: 17,228  
Updated: A Long Time Ago
